***парной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парно́й</a> (9084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пара.html>пар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">par</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fresh <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>parnóje</b> molokó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fresh milk; milk fresh from the cow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>parnóje</b> mjáso</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fresh-killed meat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hot and close, warm and damp, sultry, muggy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of air</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парна́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parnája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">dative singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парной.html>парна́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parnája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паровоз.html>парово́з</a> (4609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пара.html>пар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">par</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-воз</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-voz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to transport</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паровоз.html>парово́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parovóz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паровоз.html>парово́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паровоз.html>парово́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паровоз.html>парово́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>steam locomotive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any locomotive</li></ol>

<li>fallow

***паром.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паром.html>паром</a> (7047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pormъ</i>. This is an instance in which the vowel reduction <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is reflected in spelling: the expected spelling is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поро́м</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poróm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паром.html>паро́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paróm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паром.html>паро́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паром.html>паро́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паром.html>паро́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ferry</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пароходик.html>парохо́дик</a> (31208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пароход.html>парохо́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paroxód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***парочка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парочка.html>па́рочка</a> (5924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пара.html>па́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pára</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-очка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-očka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***партийность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:партийность.html>парти́йность</a> (24449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">partíjnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийность.html>парти́йность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">partíjnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийность.html>парти́йности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийность.html>парти́йности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийность.html>парти́йностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> party affiliation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> party spirit, partisanship</li>
<li>occurrence of party principles <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in literature or art</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йный</a> (8543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́ртий-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pártij-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">partíjnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> party</li>
<li>loyal to the party line</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">partíjnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йных</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йная</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>party member</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>партия</a> (509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">partia</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Partie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">partie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pártija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртий</a></b>)

<ol><li>party (political group)</li>
<li>lot, batch, consignment, parcel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> detachment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> part</li>
<li>game, set, match</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партнер.html>партнёр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">partnjór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***парус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>па́рус</a> (5652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">парусъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parusŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin. Either to be connected to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Livonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Livonian language">Livonian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="liv">pūŗaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">bura</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">bùrė</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φᾶρος, φάρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phâros, pháros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">large cloth, spread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, for which latter compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксус</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úksus</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vinegar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́рдус</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párdus</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, known Greek borrowings.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парусник.html>па́русник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">párusnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парусник.html>па́русника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парусник.html>па́русники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парусник.html>па́русников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sailing ship <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of ship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b>,  Андрей Троицкий,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутка.html>Раскру́тка</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=n_5gCwAAQBAJamp;lpg=PT78amp;dq=%22%D0%BF%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%83%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA%22amp;pg=PT78v=onepageamp;q=%22%D0%BF%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%83%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Девяткин <a href = vnd.unilang:подойти.html>подошёл</a> бли́же <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окну́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>лист</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́нему</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>морю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шёл</a> трехмачтовый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:парусник.html>па́русник</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:алый.html>а́лые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наполнять.html>наполня́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Devjatkin podošel blíže k oknú, razvernúl list. Po sínemu morju šól trexmačtovyj <b>párusnik</b>, ályje parusa napolnjál véter.</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sailfish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">butterfly</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> swallowtail</li></ol>

***парусный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парусный.html>па́русный</a> (18718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>па́рус</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парусный.html>па́русный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">párusnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sail, sailing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парусный.html>па́русное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>párusnoje</b> súdno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sailing ship</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парусный.html>па́русная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>párusnaja</b> lódka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sailboat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парусный.html>па́русный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорт.html>спорт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>párusnyj</b> sport</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sailing <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sport</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">sailing sport</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
